    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;">Item 8.01 &#8211; Other Events.</div>

    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>

    <div style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 36pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">On June 8, 2023, AngioDynamics, Inc. issued a press release announcing the sale of its dialysis product portfolio and BioSentry tract sealant system
      biopsy product to Merit Medical Systems, Inc.</div>

    <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br />
    </div>

    <div style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 36pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">A copy of the press release is attached hereto as Exhibit 99.1 and is incorporated herein by reference.</div>

<body bgcolor="#ffffff" style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; text-align: left; color: #000000;">
  <font style="font-size: 10pt;"> </font>
  <hr noshade="noshade" align="center" style="height: 4px; color: #000000; background-color: #000000; text-align: center; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; border: none;">
  <div style="text-align: right;"><font style="font-weight: bold; font-size: 10pt;">Exhibit 99.1</font><font style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
    </font></div>
  <div style="text-align: left;"><font style="font-weight: bold;"> </font><font style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
    </font>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-size: 10pt;"><img width="275" height="38" src="image0.jpg"></div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;">PRESS RELEASE</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">Investor Contact:</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
    </div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">AngioDynamics, Inc.</div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">Stephen Trowbridge, Executive Vice President &amp; CFO</div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">(518) 795-1408</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
    <div style="text-align: center; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;">AngioDynamics Announces Sale of Dialysis Product Portfolio and BioSentry Product to Merit Medical Systems for $100 Million</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
    <div style="text-align: center; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-style: italic;">Announces preliminary Fiscal Year 2023 net sales in the range of $338 million to $339 million</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 12pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">Latham, New York, June 8, 2023 </font><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold;">&#8211;</font><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> AngioDynamics, Inc. (NASDAQ: ANGO), a leading and transformative medical technology company focused on
        restoring healthy blood flow in the body&#8217;s vascular system, expanding cancer treatment options and improving quality of life for patients, today announced that it has completed the sale of its Dialysis product portfolio and BioSentry Tract Sealant
        System Biopsy product to Merit Medical Systems, Inc. for $100 million in cash.</font></div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
    </div>
    <div style="text-align: left; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">The transaction consists of AngioDynamics&#8217; DuraFlow&#8482;, DuraMax<sup style="vertical-align: text-top; line-height: 1; font-size: smaller;">&#174;</sup>, Evenmore<sup style="vertical-align: text-top; line-height: 1; font-size: smaller;">&#174;</sup>, Schon XL<sup style="vertical-align: text-top; line-height: 1; font-size: smaller;">&#174;</sup>, Trio-CT<sup style="vertical-align: text-top; line-height: 1; font-size: smaller;">&#174;</sup> and Vaxel
      Plus Hemodialysis Catheter brands, and BioSentry&#8482; Tract Sealant System Biopsy brand.&#160; This combined portfolio of products contributed approximately $32 million in sales in AngioDynamics&#8217; Fiscal Year 2023.</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
    </div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 12pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">AngioDynamics intends to use net proceeds to eliminate its existing debt and support
        further strategic investments in growth and profitability.&#160; </font><font style="font-size: 10pt;">The divested assets are included in the Company&#8217;s Med Device Business and do not have a significant amount of direct costs.&#160; As a result, the
        transaction will be dilutive to adjusted earnings per share and is expected to be slightly dilutive to corporate gross margins.</font></div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
    </div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">&#8220;I am excited to announce this divestiture, which supports our focus on our high-growth Med Tech platforms.&#160; While this deal divests strong product lines, we&#8217;re pleased
      with the value we&#8217;ve received for these assets, as the transaction strengthens our balance sheet and better positions us to focus on driving growth in our NanoKnife, Mechanical Thrombectomy and Auryon businesses,&#8221; commented Jim Clemmer, President and
      Chief Executive Officer of AngioDynamics.&#160; &#8220;This is another significant step in our transformation, and finding an excellent partner to take on these leading dialysis and biopsy assets allows our team to more tightly align around the Company&#8217;s core
      strategic platforms.&#8221;</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
    </div>
    <div style="clear: both; margin-top: 10pt; margin-bottom: 10pt;" class="BRPFPageBreakArea">
      <div style="page-break-after: always;" class="BRPFPageBreak">
        <hr noshade="noshade" style="margin: 4px 0px; width: 100%; border-width: 0; height: 2px; color: #000000; background-color: #000000; clear: both;"></div>
    </div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">Mr. Clemmer added, &#8220;Through this acquisition, Merit gains well-recognized and dependable products from our Med Device portfolio that clinicians trust to provide the best
      patient care. We are pleased that Merit, a leading global manufacturer and marketer of healthcare technology, is acquiring our Dialysis brands and BioSentry biopsy product.&#8221;</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
    </div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">Management expects the Company&#8217;s net sales for its recently completed fiscal year ended May 31, 2023, inclusive of the Dialysis Product Portfolio and BioSentry product, to
      be in the range of $338 million to $339 million.&#160; AngioDynamics will report fiscal year results and provide guidance for the 2024 fiscal year in early July.</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
    </div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">UBS Investment Bank is serving as financial advisor, and Cadwalader, Wickersham &amp; Taft is serving as legal advisor to AngioDynamics. Piper Sandler is serving as
      financial advisor, and Parr Brown Gee &amp; Loveless is serving as legal advisor to Merit Medical Systems.</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
    </div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;">About AngioDynamics, Inc.</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
    </div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 12pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: rgb(34, 34, 34);">AngioDynamics is a leading and transformative medical technology company focused on
        restoring healthy blood flow in the body&#8217;s vascular system,</font><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> expanding cancer treatment options,</font><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: rgb(34, 34, 34);"> and improving quality of life for patients.</font></div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
    </div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 12pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: rgb(34, 34, 34);">The Company&#8217;s innovative technologies and devices are chosen by talented physicians
        in </font><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">fast-growing healthcare markets to treat unmet patient needs. For more information, visit </font><u><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">www.angiodynamics.com</font></u><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">.</font></div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
    </div>
